                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 南加州華人買買買賣賣賣
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 📢 每天請勿連續PO文，一天PO一次，否則一律刪除 📢📢 🈲請勿將個人網站或他人網站PO在本版 （除非管理團隊同意） 📢📢📢 🈲不允許放微信，LINE .FACEBOOK連結. （除非管理團隊同意） 📢📢📢📢 禁止在本團販賣假貨.否則一律刪除。 買家如果有任何問題請先跟賣家私下溝通。如果賣家沒有反應或態度不好可以通知團主，或管理員。本團不歡迎筆戰，我希望大家可以快快樂樂完成彼此交易。 如果我看到一些筆戰是雙方沒有妥協好就出來反應我會立刻刪除 （請發表意見前先通知版主） 只要是第一位喊的人就有優先權（私詢喊me的人不算）買主me，我要了以後請馬上pm賣主，如果沒有馬上pm賣主，下一位補上，第一位喊me的人請自己私詢賣家如何取貨，賣家如果急需要把產品賣出，請註明先到先得等清楚說明免得引起爭議。 如果你對賣家產品沒有興趣，請勿參與引起爭議，這𥚃是買賣團，希望大家了解，買賣是雙方你情我願，謝謝。 本團只是提供買賣的一個平台，版主及管理者努力確保版內交易的安全但對版內po金錢交易不負任何責任，如果發生法律糾紛，本平台及經營者及管理員不負任何責任。 📢📢📢📢📢 最近很多人投訴，明明第一個先me了但賣主確説賣掉了，再次告之賣家，為了維護買賣雙方的權利和免得大家浪費彼此時間，買家可以跟版主和管理員投訴，二次以上將退此賣家出團，沒有警告喲！ 同樣的，買家me之後習慣性pass,賣家可以像版主或管理員投訴，兩次以上會直接請出本版。 📢📢📢📢📢📢 凡是要賣東西的團友，如果覺得我這𥚃可以幫助你賣的掉的，請勿到別團賣相同的產品，如果你在我團賣又跑到別團賣，對不起我一律直接封鎖，大家可以檢舉。（相信我，每團的人都差不多一樣的人在看，實在不想再聽到一大堆人私密我說賣家到處po文，自己先me但賣主在別團先賣掉等等） 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 版主在此鄭重聲明！所有商家如果要登廣告請與版主連絡。 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 為了防止洗版太快，或有違反版規文出現，（色情，騙人廣告等等） 本團會在24小時以內審查，核格通過以後馬上會批准post ，如果沒有按照版規，我們是不會批准的。 版主與各管理員將花更多心思維護本團，請大家瞭解我們努力，再次告知：請勿同步post 到他團，一但有人檢舉直接刪除，封鎖，謝謝大家 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 Updated 各位賣家請注意 請勿連續推自己產品上來超過二個以上，如超過二個以上，我們會刪除 買賣是雙方自由，本網站不負任何責任。 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 Updated 6/29/16 各位賣家，請把post文儘可能放在一起，價格的地方請勿放Free(如果是免費送，可以）如果是有不同產品請把最低價格放在價格欄內，在產品說明的部分，請一一將價格寫在上面，請不要寫pm我問價格等等，如果不符規定，將不會批准po文，謝謝。凡是po文連續超過二個以上我們都會刪除，請把己賣出的po文刪除而不是只是sold ，因為大家還是可以找到你己賣出的po文. Update 7/6/16 感謝所有的團友支持南加州華人買買買賣賣賣為了給買家更多的保障！☺️ 所有團購賣家將會採取註冊會員制！ 即日起本團所有團購賣家必須註冊會員 （只有團購賣家） 👍報名表格請pm管理團隊 開團注意事項: 1.商品名稱 2.商品內容 3.團購價格 4.開團日期 5.結團日期 6.取貨日期 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 各位賣家請注意 1.賣家必須在24小時以內與買家連絡.(買家也請跟賣家連絡.可以在po文內告知以pm你） 2.賣家商品銷售價格請勿坐地起價，一定要標實際價格 3.如果賣家超過5次投訴，將記警告一次..3次警告將會取消資格團購賣家資格 4.賣家請註明價格，取貨地點請賣家自己私密買家，不需要po出來。 5.買家如果訂貨，刻意消失，不與賣連絡說明原因，賣家檢舉，一律退團處份。 📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢📢 歡迎加入 https://www.facebook.com/groups/1522378538055034/ https://www.facebook.com/groups/668068919928506/ 南加州華人寵物交流團 https://www.facebook.com/groups/685232844883910/ https://www.facebook.com/groups/1582075652034403/ https://www.facebook.com/groups/1771095279774270/

It is rude, and unfair to the seller. * Include where you are located, asking price, and the description of item. * Seller type "sale pending" when arrangements are made. * Sellers PLEASE delete photos when items sold* * Send PM's when arranging pickups. * If you have a conflict of some sort with another person, please contact me, or one of the other future admins. We will do our very best, to resolve the problem. * Please becareful with your purchase, as this is a virtual yard sale. Items may be a fake, so please do your research. *UPDATE: IF YOU ARE POSTING YOUR ITEMS ON OTHER SITES, PLEASE PUT CROSS POSTED IN YOUR AD, SO OTHERS KNOW THAT IT'S BEING ADVERTISED IN OTHER PLACES.                  Garage sale online for local San Fernando valley people. Rule ZERO: DO NOT SELL WEAPONS. I will delete and block you from joining again and turn you into the Facebook police (yes that does exist) On a happier note: Simply post a picture and list the item you are selling, how much you want and where pick-up is. You may set a firm price, negotiable or even make an auction. The first person who says that they are interested in a firm or negotiable item has first dibs and so forth. If they choose to pass it's on to the next person. If you are interested in an item as first come - the seller will PM (private message) you. You have to check your "others" folder in your inbox. If you can not agree upon a PU (pick up) time and date then the seller may move on to the next person. If the seller has a specific date they need the item gone by -THEY MUST LIST THIS IN THE AD. The last person to bid before the auction is over is the winner regardless of the amount. If you are the winner… you must buy the item. Do not bid if you have no intention on buying. *NOTIFICATION SETTINGS can be changed by going to the drop down menu *ABSOLUTELY NO SCAMS *PLEASE DO NOT POST YOUR AD MULTIPLE TIMES A WEEK This will result in being removed from the group. It is not okay to "clog up" the group page with the same ad every day. If you simply comment on your ad saying "item still available" it will bump your ad to the top of the page. IF YOU BUMP YOUR AD MORE THAN TWICE A WEEK YOU WILL BE REMOVED FROM THE GROUP AND WILL NOT BE PERMITTED TO JOIN AGAIN. *IF YOU HAVE MULTIPLE ITEMS make an album! Do not clog up the entire page with your items. *DO NOT POST ANY PERSONAL ADDRESSES Failure to do so will result in your post being deleted and/or being removed from the group - if you want someone to PU an item from your place of residence that is your business and you can PM the purchaser of your item. HAVE RESPECT, DO NOT CUSS or BELITTLE ANYONE. If you can not follow this simple rule, you will be PERMANENTLY REMOVED from the group. - No inappropriate items or services listed - Must live in SCV, be from SCV, or visit SCV often IF ITEM HAS BEEN SOLD DELETE PHOTO AND AD. Please understand that the admin of this group has a life outside of Facebook. Please DO NOT expect an immediate response to your issue.

When people complain here it just starts drama and grows anger. It also doesn't accomplish anything to complain here as we are not the 99 cent only store itself, we are a fan group. Let's just have fun and enjoy the hunt for those bargains!                 <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Weird Secondhand Finds That Just Need To Be Shared
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This group was created as a place for the founders to share the wacky things they find with friends and family, so we’d have a place to archive them, like some sort of strange museum. We expected to have a grand total of about a dozen members, but we welcome all you party crashers too! Share the odd, unusual, and wonderful pieces that you come across whilst thrifting, visiting yard sales, estate sales, antique stores, etc. We even accept items you inherited or found while renovating! But, this group is not for posting good deals. In fact you do not have to have purchased the items you post at all, they just need to be weird secondhand things you feel others in the group would enjoy seeing. If we feel your item is a good fit to the content we’re curating, we’ll approve it. If your post isn’t approved, just keep hunting for something new to post in the future. We review a thousand post submissions every day and simply not everything can or will be approved. Don’t get discouraged! This is a place for lighthearted fun and shenanigans. We expect you to err on the side of kindness in all of your interactions within the group. If you can’t play nice with the other kids, then you don’t get to play in our sandbox. That being said, the group is actually geared towards adults and as such you will see things like swearing, items made from animal parts, items with death themes, etc. If you find these things upsetting then this group may not be a good fit for you. Guidelines for posting: All posts must be approved by an admin. As of January 2019 admin will no longer be answering questions about why posts were not approved. The posting guidelines can be found pinned in the announcements section and following them will help to get your post approved, but there is never a guarantee. May the odds be ever in your favor!

It has further info on ticket guidelines, lost and found items, and community pitchforking. ––––– TERMS OF USE This outlines what type of sharing are allowed and what can be removed by us. It is designed to help keep ravExchange a welcoming place and to help us keep everyone safe. Your access to and use of ravExchange conditioned on your acceptance of and compliance with these terms of use. We reserve the right to: • refuse or revoke member privileges to anyone • delete posts and comments without warning if a violation occurs • issue a ban or removal without warning if a violation occurs • ban anyone who disrespect our team members without warning • make decisions as needed to preserve the peace within the community Prohibited items include but not limited to: • scamming • flaking • auctioning/bidding tickets • promoting of any kind: ambassadors, products/services, self-promo, invite codes, guest lists without permission, ride share codes, funding, living social, contests, surveys, external links, etc. • drug-related discussions and/or illegal activities • scalping - selling large quantities and/or for commercial reasons • fake accounts and/or duplicated accounts • hostility, harassment, seven-isms, etc. • spamming of any kind: hijacking original posts, posting excessively, irrelevant content/links, post disregarding rules, affiliate offers, random articles, controversial posts, surveys, school-related items, etc. • soliciting members to buy tickets from any third-party platforms. Any member guilty of the above will result in a ban. This includes any form of media (e.g. videos) Please report to us if you have any questions, concerns, or issues to our team. ––––– RESOURCES Support Portal: ravexchange.com Quick Guide to Buying: ravexchange.com/buyerawareness Verified Scammer Records: https://bit.ly/1TUsDsm Free Ticket Check: https://ravexchange.com/verify ––––– We now offer advertisement space, with selected advertisers, to bring you useful and relevant information.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a virtual yard sale. Sales and purchases are like yard sale items that you own. RULES: All posts must have picture, description, price, location. Posts can be from any city, but all transactions must be made in Bellflower or Lakewood unless both parties agree to meet in surrounding location. Posts must be in english first, then any other language after. Please pick up items at specified time and location. The seller only has to hold item for 12 hours then seller can move on to next person in line. If item is sold or pending a sale, please post "sale pending" or delete post if sold. Make sure you have exact change when picking up and selling items. If you are not a resident of Bellflower, you must let the buyer know and you can make arrangements to meet. Do not post same picture more than once per day. Dupilcate posts are not allowed. Delete prior post before reposting. Repeat offenders will have posts deleted and may be removed from the group. ******** THESE RULES ARE FOR LEGAL REASONS: NO PORNOGRAPHY NO ALCOHOL NO TOBACCO NO DRUGS (OF ANY KIND, INCLUDING ALL MEDICINES, VITAMINS, CREAMS, ETC.) NO FIREARMS OR OTHER WEAPONS. NO SALE OF PETS or ANIMALS NO BABY FORMULA OR FOOD NO FOOD OF ANY KIND, UNLESS YOU HAVE A BUSINESS PERMIT TO SELL IT. ******** NO OUT OF STATE POSTS NO LINKS OUTSIDE OF FACEBOOK NO POLITICS NO SPAM NO DRAMA OR PERSONAL ATTACKS/RUDENESS, LET'S BE ADULTS NO SOLICITATIONS OF INSURANCE, REAL ESTATE, DIET SUPPLEMENTS or PLANS, RECRUITING FOR ONLINE SALES NO SALES OF USED/OPEN MAKEUP NO STORES, THIS IS A VIRTUAL YARDSALE! People can message you for any information but not to skip someone ahead of them. Phone numbers and addresses are to be PM (private message) for safety reasons. Also, if people are shady please do not hesitate to tell me and I will remove them. If it sounds fishy... DO NOT meet up with them. Please be careful! Group members are not screened and we are not responsible in any way for other people nor is facebook liable for these people. Take someone with you when you are meeting, NEVER go alone. Posts 30 days and older are deleted, if you have items still available, please "bump" (bring up my post) your post. PLEASE BE CONSIDERATE OF THE RULES Thank you for being a part of this group...happy selling/buying!

There is no warning for such violations. You will be deleted and permanently blocked. No more than 3 posts and/or bumps per person per day. Please be considered to other members and limit your posts. Never go alone to anyone's home or give your telephone or cell number in the public group. Make sure to Private Message the other party when dealing with the final end of sale for the details. If your item has a defect or is damaged, let people know. This could apply to a car with a mechanical problem, or a phone with a bad ESN. -NO SELLING FOOD STAMPS. Nuff’ said. Get some class. -NO ADVERTISING OTHER GROUPS. Did you decide to start your own group similar to this one? Cool, but don’t try to recruit members here. -IF YOU BLOCK AN ADMIN, YOU GET BANNED. No warnings. Trying to hide your activity means you are doing something that’s not allowed.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 theXchange is the SAFEST ticket group on Facebook for music lovers to buy and sell concert tickets, without the stress of dealing with scammers and fake tickets. We spend 3-4 hours a day vetting people looking to join but we are a very small team and the occasional scammer WILL slip through. Better than groups who don’t vet at all or event pages where 90% of people are scammers though :) Tickets sold on this group can be of any genre and any city. You can use the "search this group" functionality to find a specific show. Any invalid tickets being sold and bought here will be dealt with seriously. We will investigate the situation, and if deemed necessary steps will be taken including removal of the member and possible legal actions. In situations where you are unsure of the buyer/seller, we suggest using PayPal goods and services. There is a 2.9% +$0.30 fee attached to it, but it is the safest way to buy tickets from strangers. Please read all of the rules as well as our: TERMS OF USE This outlines what type of sharing is allowed and what can be removed by theXchange. It is designed to help keep theXchange a safe yet welcoming place. Your use of theXchange is based on your acceptance of and compliance with these terms of use. We reserve the right to: • refuse or revoke member privileges to anyone • delete posts and comments without warning if a violation occurs • issue a ban or removal without warning if a violation occurs • ban anyone who disrespects our team members without warning • make decisions as needed to preserve the peace within the community theXchange is not responsible for the outcome of ANY transactions that take place in our group. We DO NOT guarantee ANY transactions. Prohibited items include but not limited to: • scamming • flaking • auctioning/bidding tickets • promotion of any kind: ambassadors, products/services, self-promo, invite codes, guest lists without permission, ride share codes, funding, contests, surveys, external links, etc. • drug-related discussions and/or illegal activities • fake accounts and/or duplicated accounts • hostility, harassment, seven-isms, etc. • spamming of any kind: hijacking original posts, posting excessively, irrelevant content/links, post disregarding rules, affiliate offers, random articles, controversial posts, surveys, school-related items, etc. • soliciting members to join other groups buy tickets from any third-party platforms. Any member guilty of the above will result in a ban. This includes any form of media (e.g. videos). We are brought to you by your friendly music curators Rock With This. Find your new favorite song today at www.rockwiththis.com. Thank you and enjoy!

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 So Cal Antiques, Vintage, Handmade, Home Décor
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 ********Group Rules******Please Read********** So Cal Group Rules: 1. BE RESPECTFUL. 2. Post a detailed description. Please include WHAT the item is, WHERE the item is located and the ASKING PRICE. No general posting about your shop, estate sale, or antique mall space; if you want to promote it, choose a SPECIFIC ITEM/ITEMS and use that as the basis for your post. Any post lacking the specified requirements will be removed. 3. Bumping allowed! (commenting on your post to bring it back to the top). Refer back to rule #1 with this, though, and please be respectful when bumping your own posts. 4. Please mark your posts “sold” when they sell: we like seeing your success! But do delete within 24 hours to keep the group from locking up with too many posts. 5. If you choose to negotiate a lower price with a seller do not do so in the post. All negotiations need to be done in a private message. 6. If you block an admin you will be deleted. Admins need to be able to comment when necessary on anything that’s posted. 7. No advertising of services, other Facebook selling exchanges, or non-vintage items. All listings must refer to a specific item or items for sale. 8. The first person who calls “interested” on an item should be approached to purchase it within the selling guidelines set by the poster. For example, if the poster says, “No holds, Paypal accepted,” then the first person should be invited to pay by Paypal. If the seller is making appointments to show the item, that person should be offered the opportunity to see it first. But if that person is unwilling or unable to commit to the seller's requirement immediately, the seller is allowed at his or her discretion to move on to the next person. There is no set time frame they must wait. If you want it, be available and ready to buy it. Please note that cross posted items may sell on other groups before you get your chance to buy, whether you were first here or not. We have no control over that. 9. We understand mistakes happen. If you violate any of these rules, we will, if possible, give you an opportunity to correct your listing before we delete it. But we do reserve the right to delete listings or members at any time without notice if we feel it’s appropriate. ----------------------------------------------------

                 This site is for the residents of the San Gabriel Valley and surrounding areas to post items they want to sell, buy, or trade.                  Shoe Game Los Angeles TWO (Buy | Sell | Trade)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to Shoe Game Los Angeles FB Page: ShoeGameLA Twitter: ShoeGameLA IG: ShoeGame.LA Group: https://www.facebook.com/groups/shoegameLA/ Page :https://www.facebook.com/shoegameLA/?ref=bookmarks Instagram: https://www.instagram.com/shoegame.la/ Understand: Please take the time to read the rules before posting in the group. Thank you and enjoy your stay in "ShoeGame LA." Please note policy may change at any given time that fits the group best interests. Submitting a post: Please state if the shoes are for sale and/or for trade. Pictures must be tagged with physical name and current date. In your description, you may state the following" Name of shoe: Condition of shoe: Size of Shoe: Asking price of shoe: Location of seller: Contact number of seller: Things to know: (ex: flaws, pick up only, meet up halfway, ETC.) Please tag your pictures at all times. All members must tag their pictures with a physical name tag. A perfect example would be writing your name on a piece of paper and adding it in the same picture as your shoes. Other forms of tags that are welcome are printed name tag, business name card, custom tags, ETC. Most tags will be allowed as long as deliver clarity and visibility within the naked eye. Personalized tag from other group will not be accepted for use. This rules and regulations are strictly zero enforced to avoid potential scammers from using stolen pictures, and to provide ownership to the shoes being moved in the group. Zero tolerance on offer up. All shoes that are intended on for sale must have a set price. No offer up and testing water are allowed to be used in the group at all times. No fakes, No unauthorized release, early release, variant passing as sample and grade A shoe at all time. This will warrant in an automatic banishment. In rare, cases, if the seller does not know the item(s) are variant, a warning will be issued. It suggested to play it safe by asking group members for legit check. NO Exceptions: Please understand and take note that there will be no types of gambling and/or bets allowed in the group. Again, NO EXCEPTIONS. Your Shoe, Your Price. There will be no price caps in this group. Admin will not dictate what and/or how you sell your shoe(s) for. However, its always good to price match the current market value. You as the seller will only benefit best. Respect All Members &amp; Admins: Admin in behalf of Shoe Game Los Angeles are pleasured to have everyone be a part of our network. Please respect every member and administrators in the group. If there are any conflicts between members, please contact admin by sending direct message. Be patient! Admin will respond as soon possible. By joining Shoe Game Los Angeles (Buy-Sell-trade-Payment Plan), you acknowledge that you read and fully understand the Rules of Conduct. It is assumed that you are aware of these rules and regulations. Creator: Marvin John Lopez Sasan

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Facelist LA is a Buy/Sell/Trade group for Los Angeles and surrounding cities. Browse hundreds of items posted daily while supporting your local businesses. Rules: -Buy/Sell at your own risk. -Be aware of spammers and fake profiles. Moderators do their best to remove fake profiles and spammers, but please be careful. -No illegal items (drug paraphernalia, weapons, fireworks etc) -We allow posts for animals to find new homes to responsible, caring owners interested in adopting or re-homing animals. Please be diligent and have paperwork available. If there is any discrepancy the seller or buyer is sketchy they will immediately be banned and reported to the police. -Be respectful. Rude or inappropriate content reported will be deleted and the member will be removed. -Please bump posts. Multiple posts of the same items will be deleted. *Facelist LA is not responsible for any transactions and posts and is not liable. All purchases are solely exclusive between the seller and buyer. *

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome To JDM MarketPlace JDM MarketPlace Was Created To Help Car Enthusiasts Afford Good Quality And REAL Parts! If You Have HookUps With Anything That Will Help The Community Please Go Ahead And Post Away! Wholesale Price HookUps Are A Plus! Sell Parts, Cars, Trade, Misc. If You Offer Any Kind Of Service Such As Mechanical, Photography, Painting, Supplier For Parts, And Shops Feel Free To Post Them Lets Try To Keep It As Clean As Possible. Rules Are Simple No Posting EBAY/ NO NAME Items, WHEELS ARE AN EXCEPTION No Phones And Unrated Car Parts This Isn't RADIOSHACK No Trolling No Talking SHIT BECAUSE YOU ARE BORED NO DRAMA!!! ZERO TOLERANCE FOR ANY OF IT AND UR POSTS WILL BE DELETED, Only One Warning Then You Will Be Banned, Enjoy! Racing Crews / Car Meets &amp; Greets / For Sale Ads / For Trade Ads / Advertise Your Private Business / Company MUST POST A PRICE OR YOUR POST WILL BE DELETED, No "Offer" It Will Save You And The Person That Is Interested Time. POSTING ITEMS - It is important to list an item description and price for all items listed. Photos are optional, but do help items to sell quicker. ONLY POST ONCE - Only post your item once. Duplicate items will be removed. DELETE YOUR POSTS - Please remember to delete your photos once your item has sold. To do this, find your photo in the "Photos" link at the top of the group. Once you have clicked on your photo, hover over the photo and a bar will appear at the bottom. There will be an "Options" link. Click the link and it will then give you the option to "Remove this Photo". Then you will be asked to confirm. ALL SALES FINAL - All sales are final on the site. Admin is not responsible for any transactions that take place. The buyer and seller need to work out any issues that arise. If the buyer is not happy with their purchase, they can contact the seller--but it is at the seller's discretion as to whether or not they want to refund the money for the purchase. Once money is exchanged for an item and the item is in the buyer's possession, the sale is complete. If the buyer is not happy with the item once they get it home, they are more than welcome to repost. DON'T RUIN SALES - Please do not try and "ruin" other people's sales. If you do not agree with their price or think it is too high, do not try and tell people to get the item somewhere else. Let people handle their own posts. Buyers can do their own research and price shop. Keep Your Comments Respectful! No Trolling NO DRAMA! NO SHIT TALKING 0 TOLERANCE FOR ANY OF IT Bad Rep For Flaking Will Be Humiliated And Banned, Man Up And Say Ur No Longer Interested One Thing I Do Ask Is, Make Sure You Suggest Your Friends To This Page.                 <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Hello everyone and Welcome to the group where you can buy, sell, give and trade you're items lets make this group a drama free place and lets all get along and enjoy buying and selling... PLEASE respect all members of this group! Rude and childish behavior will not be tolerated and you will be removed and BANNED! Thank You! Please follow the following guidelines when posting: When listing items please list price and If you are cross posting in different sites Please post clothing items in an album, it makes the site easier to view items Do not relist items to bring to the top. "Bumping" them will bring them to the top. Only BUMP items you are selling every 24 hours. No selling of PETS or animals SELLER: Only list authentic brands of purses or accessories. Selling fakes is against the rules. Please give buyers a reasonable time to get back to you to set up pick up.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Upland &amp; Surrounding Cities Marketplace
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Many surrounding cities limit the number of garage sales you can have per year and also has strict guidelines for such. Here, you can post pictures of the items you no longer want or need and you can sell or swap with other Upland or surrounding cities residents. Buyers beware! Items are as is and final sale, unless otherwise stated by the seller. Inspecting items before you buy is your responsibility. Post must be of items that available for immediate sale. No "taking orders". What the members see, is what they get. Please delete your post after your item(s) sell. This will keep the page and photo albums fresh with only items that are available and will alleviate any confusion. If you do not delete your posts after it's been picked up, you may be temporarily removed from the group. Members have the right to report members that fail to delete posts that are no longer available. Also, please be advised that inappropriate posts can and will be deleted by an Administrator, with the member being banned from the group. Upland Swap is not intended as a free advertisement tool for businesses. All posts containing links and/or advertisements will be deleted and the member will be permanently banned for not adhering to this policy. Upland Swap Administrators care about your health and safety. If you respond to an ad that has yet to be deleted by an administrator, you do so at your own risk. We appreciate your help in reporting any policy violator. There are no rules to how sales are to be handled. To each is own. Unfortunately no shows and "I've changed my mind" happen. Move on and if you don't want to sell to that person again, don't! It's your call! Furthermore, Upland Swap Administrators do not support and/or endorse any person or post on Upland Swap. Administrators reserves the right to delete posts and/or remove members as they see fit, without explanation. Please help build our community group and invite your friends to join Upland Swap! Administrator approval is required of all requests to join. We will add members at a time that is convenient for us. Please refrain from messaging an administrator to add your friends. They will be added when we can get to it. Upland Swap is intended for Upland residents and surrounding community members; i.e. Pomona, Claremont, La Verne, Glendora, San Dimas, Rancho Cucamonga, etc; .. Administrators cannot determine where members live/work when they request to join. It is unlikely that members will be willing to drive too far. We trust that members that do not live or work in Upland and/or its surrounding areas, that they will leave the group on their own. Lastly, we will help with any situation you need help with, however please understand that we cannot tend to Upland Swap 24/7. We will address concerns as quickly as we can. Upland Swap was created with the intent for it to run on its own. Happy swapping!
                </div>

DO NOT put people on blast in a post about any problems that arise within the group, please just contact one of the admins and the situation will be handled accordingly. 8. This is a warning so if any of this is seen you will be permanently banned. ZERO TOLERANCE. You must DELETE the item once it has sold. There is no self-promoting of any kind. This includes photographers, home businesses, etc.etc. DISCLAIMER: Members of this group participiate AT THEIR OWN RISK.                  This group is for Furniture and Household items for sellers and buyers. Mainly for sales, free giveaways, or for personal Garage Sale announcements! This group is for Orange County in California locals only. Please read below the rules before posting. Hello everyone, I am the Admin of this group. Just trying to make it easier for you to find me if you ever need to reach out. RULES NO ADVERTISING nor PROMOTING any businesses, properties, live videos, other groups, sell promotion will be blocked from the group without any warnings. No Selling or Renting houses posts under any circumstances. Please let's be kind to each other and no rude comments, after all, we all live in the same county and we are all adults. However, if I will see personal attacks from anyone, that person will be deleted from the group without any notice. There is no tolerance for fake buyers/sellers! Please be considering of others time and efforts. If someone flakes out, please report these people names to me directly with proof and I will delete them from the group. This is for both, sellers and buyers. I am sorry, but I have no tolerance for people who doesn't respect others. -Sellers, make sure you post a price and location on your selling items or your post will be deleted. -If you post your items for sale in other groups, please make sure to post " cross posted" in your post to let the buyers know. -Sellers needs to go in order of "interested" from potential buyer under sellers post comments. -If a seller is selling the item first come, first serve basis, please post that in your post. -NO AUCTIONS, no biddings. -Please consider to give enough time for a buyer to to get back to you before moving on to the next potential buyer. -If a buyer commits to the sale, please don't sell the item to anyone else unless this potential buyer doesn't fallow through. ADVERTISING: You need get approved by admin BEFORE you post. If not, you and your post can be deleted without warning. PETS No FREE or sale pets postings! OUTSIDE OC RESIDENTS This group is for OC residence. Therefore, none OC residents can't charge for any delivery fees and should be flexible about meeting anyone in OC area.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 UCI Textbooks (for You, Me, and Everybody)
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Tired of waiting for UC Irvine’s textbook buyback days? Frustrated that you only received $10 back for your $300 physics book? Our mission is to provide reasonably priced textbooks from/for UCI students. ____________________________________ Guidelines for SELLERS: 1) List the title, price, and attach a photo of the textbook. OR use this template: COURSE: TITLE: EDITION: AUTHOR(S): ISBN # HARDBACK/PAPERBACK: CONDITION: PRICE: COMMENTS: 2) Once you receive offers from potential buyers, pick a time and place to make the exchange. (I recommend the FLAGPOLES or STARBUCKS on campus.) 3) Exchange contact information to avoid miscommunication (e.g. the buyer arrives 30 minutes late because s/he was stuck in traffic). ____________________________________ Guideline for BUYERS: 1) Find the textbook you need ([CTRL + f] function). OR post the title the textbook you need and its course 2) Respond to the wall post or PM the seller. Pick a time and place to make the exchange. 3) Exchange contact information to avoid miscommunication. 4) Word of caution: Make sure to carefully review/flip through the book to ensure that it is the book that you need, and pay the seller at the location of the pickup to avoid any potential unscrupulous sellers who are dishonest. Constant vigilance! ____________________________________ Good luck! (^_^) Spread the word! Tell your friends about our Facebook group. This way, we'll gather more people and more books to fit everybody's needs. (-_-;;)
